 Actor Viju Khote, best known for his roles in Sholay and Andaz Apna Apna, passed away on Monday
 He was 77
 
 After making his silver screen debut in 1964 film Ya Malak, Viju went on to star in movies like Sholay, Qurbani, Karz, Nagina, Qayamat Se Qayamat Tak and Andaz Apna Apna among more
 
 Viju Khote is best remembered for his brief role in Sholay, in which he played an underling of Amjad Khan's Gabbar
 His character in the film spoke one of the most well-known lines in Hindi cinema: "sardar maine aap ka namak khaya hai
 " 
 In Andaz Apna Apna, he played the role of Robert and his appearance was also marked by a line of dialogue that later became famous: "galti se mistake hogaya
 " 
 He was also known for his work in popular 90s sitcom Zabaan Sambhalke, which was based on British show Mind Your Language
 
 Besides having over 300 Hindi and Marathi films to his credit, Viju Khote was also active in Marathi theater
 (via Indian Express)

 sitambar 2013 main bibisi or ek saal baad nanvabar 2014 main financial express ne likhaa he ki songdo ke karmtial spes kaa 20 pratishat bhi istamaal nahin ho sakaa he
 Your anchor does not know what is the situation right now
 tippaniyan Like Songdo, a phase of a finance city in India has been completed
 2007 main mukhyamantri ke taur par narendra modi ne isaki buniyaad rakhi thi jo 2022 main puraa hoga or puraa hone tak isamen kareeb 8 xxrep 4 0 karod rupaya lag jayega
 According to what i can understand, the Gujarat government partnered with a Mumbai company by taking wastelands and formed a new company
 nai company ne 1000 karod se zyada kii puunji lone se ugaahi or ek dhaancha taiyaar kar diya
 The gift is also like Songdo
 yahaan par centrali kooling plant he jiske zariye sari imaaraton ke taapmaana ko niyantrit kiya jayega
 There will be huge energy savings
 vaise hi sari imaaraton kaa kachra basament se ek pipe ke zariye kendriya west management plant main chalaa jayega
 The underground tunnel is built next to the roads with separate pipes to carry cold air for electricity, water, waste and AC
 china ne bhi aise kai smart city banaae hai
 Village to village zamindoz was given for smart city but no one living there now
 itani tezi se itane shahar bana diye ki zyaadaatar smart city khaali he
 These smarts have now been renamed
 inhen ghost yani bhootaha shahar kaha ja rahaa he
 What is not there, is not just man
 technology ke dam par shahar kii kshamta kaa vikaas to ho jayega magar kya shahar shahar rah jayega
 There are many questions regarding the smart city
 raajnneetik sawaal bhi hai or aarthik bhi
 JNURM was started in 2005 with a target to improve the infrastructure of cities
 kai jagah acha kaam hua he lekin kai jagahon main kaam ke naam par paisa tamaam hi hua he
 In 2012, the CAG reported that only 231 of the 1298 schemes approved under JNURM were completed
 is yojana ke tahat 65 hazaar karod se zyada kaa bajet diya gaya lekin sarkaar ne aadha se zyada paisa relies hi nahin kiya
 Every state will have at least one smart city under the new AMRUT scheme
 jis shahar yaa jagah kaa naam smart city main aayega use paanch saal ke liye har saal 100 karod kii madad milegi
 There is a debate all over the world as to what is a smart city and for whom
 china, korea or saudi main smart city banakar taiyaar bhi ho chukaa he or kai deshon main jaise rio di janerio, madrid tip ke puraane shaharon ko smart kiya ja rahaa he
 In 2008, IBM company developed the concept of smart city but now many IT and finance companies are involved in creating smart city
 ye smart city mek in india se nahin balki videshi companiyon ke sahyog se banegi
 This January, when US President Obama came to India, there was an agreement that America will help make three cities smart in India
 teen smart shahar banane main madad karegaa
 Allahabad, Ajmer and Visakhapatnam
 2014-15 ke bajet main smart city ke kareeb 7000 karod kii raashi tay karte hue kaha tha ki smart shahar bade shaharon ke satellite kii tarah basenge
 Like Navi Mumbai near Mumbai and Greater Noida near Delhi
 is tarah kai multi neshnal companiyaan ab smart city banane ke kaam main lagi hai
 Whether or not our homegrown real estate people will get a chance will know all this later
 upie sarkaar ke samay kerala ke kochi, gujarat ke ahmedabad, maharashtra ke aurangabad, haryana ke manesar, rajasthan ke khushkeda, andhrapradesh ke krishnapattan, tamilnadu ke ponneri or karnataka ke tumkur main smart city kii yojana launch kii gai thi
 In 2012, Kamal Nath announced that he would build two smart cities in each state
 iske liye upie ne jeenenyuarem ke tahat smart city ke liye 2013 ke bajet main 18500 karod kii raashi tay kii thi
 What the UPA could do in two years is not known, but now Prime Minister Modi is going ahead on the plan to build 100 smart cities
 sarkaar ek taraf gaanvon ko digital banane kii taiyaari main lagi he to duusari taraf gaanv se shahar aane waalon ke liye digital shahar bana rahi he
 All these people who will reduce India's urban population to 70 percent, will be asked by any political party, whether or not they will be eligible to live in smart city through mobile sensor
 shahar apane aap main ek vishay he
 Scholars studying it are asking that seventy percent of people in Delhi, Mumbai are of average income or are poor
 jyadatar log galiyon ke konon main apni dukaane laga lete hai, patariyon par chaat, chinia baadaam bech lete hai, ped ke neeche maaruti car ke bonut par juute se lekar kapadaa bech lete hai or aaraam se garmi ke dinon main bel to sardi ke dinon main anda bechakar ji lete hai
 Will there be a place for these people in the smart city
 kisi ko iske bare main thik se pataa nahin he or na hi hamaare raajnneetik dalon kii is par koi samaj bani he
 By the way, our builders keep launching such cities every year
 ab to bees pachis hazaar kii aabaadi vaale in privet shaharon main thane se lekar skool tak banane lage hai
 You must have seen that outside the city of builders, from a textile presser to a vegetable shop, it feeds
 kya smart city main use chance milegaa
 Can the existing cities not be much better off? vaise duniya ke kai puraane shaharon ne khud ko behatar karne ke liye 20 se 50 million dollar ke project banaae hai
 Rio de Janeiro, madrid et cetera
 (hamane ye video cisco company kii site se liya he) dakshin korea kaa smart shahar songdo he jo 2009 main launch hua tha
 Songdo is to become a finance city like Hong Kong and Singapore
 yahaan sab kuch automatic he
 From a center you can control the temperature or energy consumption of any building
 sensor se aapako mobile par sandesh aa jayega ki kab bas aane vaali he, mobile par samasya tip kiijie, sthaneey prashasan ko pataa chal jayega
 With this, the question arises in the context of India whether our governments will also change the administration and rights of the municipality for this

 enarasi ke andar koi praavdhaan nahin he ki or dharmon ke logon ko register main naa liya jaae
 People of all religions will be taken into it who are citizens of India
 isamen dharm ke aadhaar par bhedbhaav karne kaa koi prashn hi nahin he
 The NRC is a separate process and the Citizenship Ammendment Bill is a separate process
